  ✅ MATCHED (DIRECT, Score: 90): Scoutit - Jr. Data Engineer
     └ 📝 Step-by-step reasoning:
1.  **DB1 (Experience):** The job is titled 'Jr. Data Engineer' and mentions 'Jr. Data Engineers'. This implies an experience level typically below 5 years. The candidate has 3.8 years, which falls within the 0-5 year range and does not strictly require MORE than 5 years. Dealbreaker NOT triggered.
2.  **DB2 (AI/ML):** The responsibilities focus on designing, building, and maintaining data pipelines, ETL workflows, SQL queries, Python scripts for data transformation, data quality, and supporting analytics. There is no mention of designing, training, or building AI/ML models or advanced statistical/mathematical modeling. Dealbreaker NOT triggered.
3.  **DB3 (Azure/GCP without AWS):** The job mentions 'cloud platforms' generally but does not exclusively require Azure or GCP without mentioning AWS. The candidate has AWS experience, which aligns with 'cloud platforms'. Dealbreaker NOT triggered.
4.  **DB4 (Deloitte):** The hiring company is 'Scoutit', not Deloitte. Dealbreaker NOT triggered.

**Skill Alignment:**
*   **Role:** 'Jr. Data Engineer' is a direct match for the 'Data Engineer' target role and the candidate's experience level.
*   **Python:** 'Write efficient SQL queries and Python scripts for data transformation' is a direct match.
*   **SQL:** 'Write efficient SQL queries and Python scripts for data transformation' is a direct match.
*   **PySpark:** Not explicitly mentioned in the job description.
*   **AWS:** The job mentions 'cloud platforms' generally. While specific AWS tools are not listed, the candidate's AWS experience is relevant for a general cloud platform requirement.
*   **ETL/ELT:** 'designing, building, and maintaining data pipelines and ETL workflows' and 'Extract, transform, and load (ETL) data' are direct matches.
*   **Data Migration/Warehousing:** Implied by 'data integration across databases, APIs, and cloud platforms' and 'data systems', though not explicitly stated as 'data migration' or 'data warehousing'.

**Conclusion:** All dealbreakers are cleared. There is a strong direct alignment with core Data Engineering responsibilities (Python, SQL, ETL, pipelines, data quality, data integration). While specific AWS tools and PySpark aren't mentioned, the overall fit is excellent. The generic 'cloud platforms' requirement aligns well with the candidate's AWS expertise, making this a direct match rather than a potential match (as no specific non-AWS cloud platform was strictly required).
